             <div id="watch-description" class="yt-uix-expander yt-uix-expander-collapsed yt-uix-button-panel"> 
              <div id="watch-description-content"> 
               <div id="watch-description-clip"> 
                <p id="watch-uploader-info"> <strong>Published on <span id="eow-date" class="watch-video-date">Mar 5, 2014</span> </strong> </p> 
                <div id="watch-description-text"> 
                 <p id="eow-description">UC Riverside has never forgotten that it is located in the heart of Indian country, and through scholarship, research, and outreach programs, the university is helping Native communities write their histories on their own terms. <br /><br />To read the whole story, go to <a href="http://magazine.ucr.edu/522" target="_blank" title="http://magazine.ucr.edu/522" rel="nofollow" dir="ltr" class="yt-uix-redirect-link">http://magazine.ucr.edu/522</a>.</p> 
                </div>
